namespace = gray_gal

###################################################
# 2.1.2- 路线1
###################################################
country_event = {
	id = gray_gal.1
	title = NAME_Gray
	desc = gray_gal.1.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	custom_gui = gray_dialogue_window_no_option
	immediate = {
		remove_country_flag = wg_dialogue_charactor_lost_focus
		set_variable = { which = gray_dialogue_bg value = 4 }
		set_variable = { which = wg_dialogue_gray_portrait value = 3 }
	}

	option = {
		name = EMPTY_STRING
		custom_gui = wg_dialogue_click_any_button
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = gray_gal.2 }}
	}
	option = {
		name = EMPTY_STRING
		custom_gui = wg_hiding_button
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = gray_gal.35 }}
		default_hide_option = yes
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = gray_gal.43
	title = NAME_Gray
	desc = gray_gal.43.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	custom_gui = gray_dialogue_window
	custom_gui_option = wg_dialogue_button
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { which = gray_dialogue_bg value = 6 }
		set_variable = { which = wg_dialogue_gray_portrait value = 8 }
		remove_country_flag = wg_dialogue_charactor_lost_focus
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clear_variable = wg_dialogue_gray_portrait
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = gray_warship_active }}
				create_gray_warship = yes
			}
			country_event = { id = gray_origin.48 }
			country_event = { id = gray_gal.86 days = 180 random = 360 }
		}
		begin_event_chain = {
			event_chain = gray_origin_terraform_planet_chain
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gray_gal.43.a
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = gray_gal.44
	title = NAME_Gray
	desc = {
		exclusive_trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_gestalt = no
				has_authority = auth_shenhai
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = gray_storyline_control }
		}
		text = gray_gal.44.desc
	}
	desc = {
		exclusive_trigger = {
			NOR = {
				is_gestalt = no
				has_authority = auth_shenhai
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = gray_storyline_control }
		}
		text = gray_gal.44.desc.b
	}
	desc = gray_gal.44.desc.c
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	custom_gui = gray_dialogue_window
	custom_gui_option = wg_dialogue_button
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { which = gray_dialogue_bg value = 6 }
		set_variable = { which = wg_dialogue_gray_portrait value = 8 }
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = gray_gal.45 }}
	}

	option = {
		name = gray_gal.44.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_gestalt = no
				has_authority = auth_shenhai
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = refuse_storyline_talk_to_gray}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = gray_gal.44.b
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				is_gestalt = no
				has_authority = auth_shenhai
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = refuse_storyline_talk_to_gray}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = gray_gal.44.c
		trigger = { has_country_flag = refuse_storyline_talk_to_gray }
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = gray_story_affection value = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = gray_gal.44.d
		trigger = { has_country_flag = refuse_storyline_talk_to_gray }
	}
	option = {
		name = gray_gal.44.e
		trigger = { has_country_flag = refuse_storyline_talk_to_gray }
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = gray_story_affection value = -1 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = gray_gal.45
	title = NAME_Gray
	desc = gray_gal.45.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	custom_gui = gray_dialogue_window
	custom_gui_option = wg_dialogue_button
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { which = gray_dialogue_bg value = 6 }
		set_variable = { which = wg_dialogue_gray_portrait value = 2 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = refuse_storyline_talk_to_gray }
				country_event = { id = gray_gal.587 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = gray_gal.46 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gray_gal.45.a

	}
	option = {
		name = EMPTY_STRING
		custom_gui = wg_hiding_button
		default_hide_option = yes
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = gray_gal.96
	title = NAME_Player
	desc = gray_gal.96.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	custom_gui = gray_dialogue_window_no_option
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { which = gray_dialogue_bg value = 7 }
		set_variable = { which = wg_dialogue_gray_portrait value = 1 }
		set_country_flag = wg_dialogue_charactor_lost_focus
	}

	after = {
		remove_country_flag = wg_dialogue_charactor_lost_focus
	}

	option = {
		name = EMPTY_STRING
		custom_gui = wg_dialogue_click_any_button
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = gray_gal.97 }}
	}
	option = {
		name = EMPTY_STRING
		custom_gui = wg_hiding_button
		hidden_effect = { 
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = gray_storyline_control }}
				country_event = { id = gray_origin.80 }
			} else = {
				country_event = { id = gray_gal.110 }
			}
		}
		default_hide_option = yes
	}
}

				country_event = { id = gray_origin.80 }
			} else = {
				country_event = { id = gray_gal.110 }
			}
		}
		default_hide_option = yes
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = gray_gal.110
	title = NAME_Gray
	desc = gray_gal.110.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	custom_gui = gray_dialogue_window
	custom_gui_option = wg_dialogue_button
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { which = gray_dialogue_bg value = 7 }
		set_variable = { which = wg_dialogue_gray_portrait value = 5 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gray_gal.110.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = gray_storyline_control }
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = gray_gal.111 }}
		default_hide_option = yes
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = gray_storyline_control
		}
		name = gray_gal.110.b
		hidden_effect = { 
			# 小灰好感度-1
			country_event = { id = gray_gal.130 }
			change_variable = { which = gray_story_affection value = -1 }
		}
		default_hide_option = yes
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = gray_storyline_control
		}
		name = gray_gal.110.c
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = gray_gal.135 }
			change_variable = { which = gray_story_affection value = 1 }
		}
	}
}

	}

	option = {

		custom_gui = wg_dialogue_click_any_button
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = gray_gal.143 }}
	}
	option = {
		name = EMPTY_STRING
		custom_gui = wg_hiding_button
		default_hide_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { 
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = gray_storyline_control }
				country_event = { id = gray_gal.176 }
			} else = {
				country_event = { id = gray_origin.81 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	option = {

				which = gray_story_affection
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

			}
			country_event = { id = gray_gal.178 }
		}
	}

		custom_gui = wg_dialogue_click_any_button
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = gray_gal.244 }}
	}
	option = {
		name = EMPTY_STRING
		custom_gui = wg_hiding_button
		default_hide_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { 
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = gray_storyline_control }
				country_event = { id = gray_gal.245 }
			} else = {
				country_event = { id = gray_origin.82 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = NAME_Player
	desc = gray_gal.355.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	custom_gui = gray_dialogue_window_no_option
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { which = gray_dialogue_bg value = 10 }
		set_variable = { which = wg_dialogue_gray_portrait value = 1 }
		set_country_flag = wg_dialogue_charactor_lost_focus
	}

	after = {
		remove_country_flag = wg_dialogue_charactor_lost_focus
	}

	option = {
		name = EMPTY_STRING
		custom_gui = wg_dialogue_click_any_button
		hidden_effect = { 
			if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = gray_storyline_245b
						AND = {
							check_variable = { which = gray_storyline_affection value <= 2 }
							has_country_flag = gray_storyline_control
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = gray_gal.356 }
			} else = {
				country_event = { id = gray_gal.378 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EMPTY_STRING
		custom_gui = wg_hiding_button
		default_hide_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = gray_gal.534 }}
	}
}

	title = NAME_Player
	desc = gray_gal.450.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	custom_gui = gray_dialogue_window_no_option
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { which = gray_dialogue_bg value = 10 }
		set_variable = { which = wg_dialogue_gray_portrait value = 6 }
	}

	option = {
		name = EMPTY_STRING
		custom_gui = wg_dialogue_click_any_button
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = gray_gal.451 }}
	}
	option = {
		name = EMPTY_STRING
		custom_gui = wg_hiding_button
		default_hide_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = gray_gal.534 }}
	}
}

	}

country_event = {
	id = gray_gal.466
	title = EMPTY_STRING
	desc = gray_gal.466.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	custom_gui = gray_dialogue_window_no_option
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = wg_dialogue_charactor_lost_focus
		set_variable = { which = wg_dialogue_gray_portrait value = 0 }
	}

	option = {
		name = EMPTY_STRING
		custom_gui = wg_dialogue_click_any_button
		hidden_effect = { 
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { 
					NOT = { has_country_flag = gray_storyline_control }
					check_variable = { which = gray_story_affection value >= 3 }
				}}
				country_event = { id = gray_gal.467 }
			} else = {
				country_event = { id = gray_gal.471 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EMPTY_STRING
		custom_gui = wg_hiding_button
		default_hide_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = gray_gal.534 }}
	}
}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = wg_dialogue_charactor_lost_focus
	}

	option = {
		name = EMPTY_STRING
		custom_gui = wg_dialogue_click_any_button
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = gray_gal.585 }}
	}
	option = {
		name = EMPTY_STRING
		custom_gui = wg_hiding_button
		default_hide_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = gray_gal.586 }}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = gray_gal.587
	title = NAME_Gray
	desc = gray_gal.587.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	custom_gui = gray_dialogue_window_no_option
	immediate = {
		remove_country_flag = wg_dialogue_charactor_lost_focus
		set_variable = { which = wg_dialogue_gray_portrait value = 1 }
	}

	option = {
		name = EMPTY_STRING
		custom_gui = wg_dialogue_click_any_button
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = gray_gal.588 }}
	}
	option = {
		name = EMPTY_STRING
		custom_gui = wg_hiding_button
		default_hide_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = gray_gal.589 }}
	}
}

	id = gray_gal.588

	}
	option = {
		name = EMPTY_STRING
		custom_gui = wg_hiding_button
		default_hide_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = gray_gal.589 }}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = gray_gal.589
	title = NAME_Gray
	desc = gray_gal.589.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	custom_gui = gray_dialogue_window
	custom_gui_option = wg_dialogue_button

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clear_variable = wg_dialogue_gray_portrait
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = gray_warship_active }}
				create_gray_warship = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = gray_story_affection value <= -2 }}
				set_country_flag = gray_leave
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = gray_gal.86 days = 180 random = 360 }
			}
			country_event = { id = gray_origin.48 }
		}
		begin_event_chain = {
			event_chain = gray_origin_terraform_planet_chain
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gray_gal.589.a
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = gray_story_affection value = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = gray_gal.589.b
	}
	option = {
		name = gray_gal.589.c
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = { which = gray_story_affection value = -1 }
		}
	}
}
